			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">Chipotle ANNOUNCES SECOND QUARTER 2021 RESULTS</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">COMPARABLE restaurant SALES accelerate to 31.2%, RESULTING IN RECORD OPERATING PROFITABILITY</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt solid #996633 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">NEWPORT BEACH, Calf. &#x2013; July 20, 2021 &#x2013; Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) today reported financial results for its second quarter ended June 30, 2021.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Second quarter highlights, year over year: </font>
		</p>

		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> Restaurant level operating margin, adjusted net income and adjusted diluted earnings per share are non-GAAP financial measures. Reconciliations to GAAP measures and further information are set f</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">orth in the table at the end of this press release. </font>

		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk53554988"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&#x201C;Chipotle&#x2019;s second quarter results highlight the strength of our brand and our people, as we demonstrated growing momentum in </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> business," said Brian Niccol, Chairman and CEO, Chipotle. "We remain confident in our key growth strategies and believe they will help us achieve </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">our next goal of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$3 million average unit volumes with industry leading returns on invested capital that improve as we continue to add Chipotlanes. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Strong</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> restaurant level economics combined with significant </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">restaurant </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">growth should allow us to optimize earnings power for many years to come.&#x201D;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">COVID-19 and Liquidity Update:</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The health and well-being of our employees and guests continues to be our top priority. Beyond the investments made in our people, restaurants</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">upply chain, we are closely following the recommendations of the CDC and local health departm</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">ents. We have implemented and enhanced numerous protocols that</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> give our employees and guests confidence that Chipotle remains steadfast in our commitment to keep them safe as </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">capacity restrictions ease and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">in-restaurant </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">ordering and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">dining</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">As of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">June 30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, 2021, Chipotle continues to maintain a strong financial</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> position with </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">nearly </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$1.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> billion in cash, investments and restricted cash, and no debt</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. We also have access to a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">00 million untapped credit facility. Our financial strength gives us the opportunity to make on-going strategic investments in our people, business, and communities, which we believe will benefit us for years to come. </font>

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>

		</p>

</div>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Results for the three months ended </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">June</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">: &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Revenue in the second quarter was $1.9 billion, an increase of 38.7% compared to the second quarter of 2020 and includes a 31.2% increase in comparable restaurant sales. We believe on-going strength in digital sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, the strong recovery of in-restaurant sales, positive customer reception to our new menu items, and lapping the peak of the pandemic</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">from last year </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">contributed to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter revenue growth. For Q3, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">while uncertainty still exists with the potential impact of COVID-19, as well as the pace of the economic recovery, if the current trends continue, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">we expect our comparable restaurant sales to be in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">low </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">to mid </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">d</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">ouble-digits</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> range.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Digital sales grew 10.5% year over year to $916.5 million and represented 48.5% of sales. A little more than half of the digital sales were from order ahead transactions as guests increasingly appreciate both the value and convenience offered by this channel, as well as the added convenience of more Chipotlanes.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">We opened 56 new restaurants during the second quarter including one relocation, and closed </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">five</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> restaurants, bringing the total restaurant count to 2,853. During the quarter, 45 of the 56 new restaurants included a Chipotlane. These formats continue to perform very well and are helping enhance guest access and convenience, as well as increase new restaurant sa</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">les, margins, and returns. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Food, beverage and packaging costs in the second quarter were 30.4% of revenue, a decrease of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">nearly 300</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> basis points compared to the second quarter of 2020. The decrease was primarily due to the benefit of menu price increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> as well as lower beef prices, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">partially offset by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">higher </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">costs associated with </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">new menu items, like quesadillas, and, to a lesser extent, avocado costs</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin was 24.5%, an increase from 12.2% in the second quarter of 2020. The improvement was driven primarily by leverage from comparable restaurant sales including menu price increases, lower promotional activity as well as lower beef prices</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> partially offset by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">higher </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">costs associated with</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> new menu items, wage inflation for one month of the second quarter, and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> avocados</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">General and administrative expenses for the second quarter were $146.0 million on a GAAP basis, or $119.2 million on a non-GAAP basis, excluding $23.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million for a modification to 2018 performance shares to account for the unplanned effects of COVID-19, $2.1 million </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">of certain </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">legal </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">expenses, and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> $1.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million of transformation expense</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">s. GAAP and non-GAAP general and administrative expenses for the second quarter of 2021 also include underlying general and administrative expenses totaling $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">92.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, $2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million of non-cash stock compensation, and $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">4.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million related to higher bonus accruals as well as payroll taxes on equity vesting and stock option exercises. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The GAAP effective income tax rate for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter was 23.7%, which is lower than our expected effective income tax rate for the full year 2021, due to elevated excess tax benefits related to option exercises and equity vesting in the second quarter. On a non-GAAP basis, the 2021 second quarter effective tax rate was 22.4%.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Net income for the second quarter was $188.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, or $6.60 per diluted share, an increase from $8.2 million, or $0.29 per diluted share, in the second quarter of 2020. Excluding the impact of PSU modifications, restaurant asset impairment and closure costs, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">legal proceeding costs, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and corporate restructuring expenses, adjusted net income was $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">212.8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million and adjusted diluted earnings per share was $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">7.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">6.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">During the quarter, our Board of Directors approved the investment of up to an additional $200 million, exclusive of commissions, to repurchase shares of our common stock, subject to market conditions. Including this repurchase authorization, $208.5 million was available as of June 30, 2021. The repurchase authorization may be modified, suspended, or discontinued at any time. We repurchased $145.3 million of stock at an average price</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per share</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> of $1,4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">08</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> during the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">More information will be available in our Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q, which will be filed with the SEC by the end of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">July</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Definitions</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> following definitions apply to these terms as used throughout this release:</font>
		</p>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Comparable restaurant sales, or sales comps, and comparable restaurant transactions, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represent the change in period-</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">over-period total revenue or transactions for restaurants in operation for at least 13 full calendar months.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Average restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">refer to the average trailing 12-month food and beverage revenue for restaurants in operation for at least 12 full calendar months.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<a name="_Hlk74719682"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represents total revenue less direct restaurant operating costs, expressed as a percent of total revenue.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Digital sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> represent food and beverage revenue generated through the Chipotle website, Chipotle app or third-party delivery aggregators. Digital sales exclude revenue deferrals associated with Chipotle Rewards. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Conference Call Details</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">will</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> host a conference call to discuss </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> financial results on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Tues</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">day, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">July 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, at 4:30 PM Eastern time.&nbsp; </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">conference</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> call can be accessed live over the phone by dialing 1-888-317-6003 or for international callers by dialing 1-412-317-6061 and use code: </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">8008658</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The call will be webcast live from the company's website on the investor relations page at ir.chipotle.com/events. An archived webcast will be available approximately one hour after the end of the call.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Chipotle</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) is cultivating a better world by serving responsibly sourced, classically-cooked, real food with wholesome ingredients without artificial colors, flavors or preservatives. Chipotle had over 2,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">85</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">0 restaurants as of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">June 30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, France and Germany and is the only restaurant company of its size that owns and operates all its restaurants. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle is ranked on the Fortune 500 and is recognized on the 2021 lists for Forbes&#x2019; America&#x2019;s Best Employers and Fortune&#x2019;s Most Admired Companies. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">With </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">nearly 102,000 employees passionate about providing a great guest experience, Chipotle is a longtime leader and innovator in the fo</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">od industry. Chipotle is committed to making its food more accessible to everyone while continuing to be a brand with a demonstrated purpose as it leads the way in digital, technology and sustainable business practices. For more information or to place an order online, visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#C08C19;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WWW.CHIPOTLE.COM</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>

		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">Certain statements in this press release are forward-looking statements as defined in the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, including statements about our future cash flow, new restaurant development plans and future long-term prospects. We use words such as &#x201C;anticipate&#x201D;, &#x201C;believe&#x201D;, &#x201C;could&#x201D;, &#x201C;should&#x201D;, &#x201C;may&#x201D;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;"> &#x201C;approximately&#x201D;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;"> &#x201C;estimate&#x201D;, &#x201C;expect&#x201D;, &#x201C;potential&#x201D;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;"> &#x201C;intend&#x201D;, &#x201C;project&#x201D;, &#x201C;target&#x201D;, and similar terms and phrases, including references to assumptions, to identify forward-looking statements. The forward-looking statements in this press release are based on currently available operating, financial and competitive information available to us as of the date of this release and we assume no obligation to update these forward-looking statements. These statements are subject to risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from those described in the statements, including but not limited to: the ongoing adverse effect of the novel coronavirus (COVID-19) pandemic on our guest traffic, restaurant sales and operating costs as a result of actions we have taken in response to the coronavirus, including closing some restaurants, ending dine in service at some restaurants while continuing to offer only takeout and/or delivery, modifying work hours at some restaurants, extending enhanced benefits to employees working during and/or impacted by the coronavirus, increasing compensation for restaurant employees, purchasing masks, gloves and additional sanitation supplies and services and delaying the construction of new restaurant openings; risks that the impact of the coronavirus pandemic will continue for a long duration and may require a more drastic response, such as closing all or most restaurants; risks of food safety and food-borne illnesses and other health concerns about our food; risks associated with our reliance on certain information technology systems and potential failures or interruptions; privacy and cyber security risks related to our acceptance of electronic payments or electronic processing of confidential customer or employee information</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">, including through our digital app;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;"> the impact of competition, including from sources outside the restaurant industry; the increasingly competitive labor market and our ability to attract and retain qualified employees; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">the financial impact of increasing our average hourly wage to $15.00; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">the impact of federal, state or local government regulations relating to our employees, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">employment practices, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">restaurant design and construction, and the sale of food or alcoholic beverages; our ability to achieve our planned growth, such as the availability of suitable new restaurant sites; increases in ingredient and other operating costs due to our Food With Integrity philosophy, tariffs or trade restrictions and supply shortages; the uncertainty of our ability to achieve expected levels of comparable restaurant sales due to factors such as changes in consumers' perceptions of our brand, including as a result of actual or rumored food safety concerns or other negative publicity, decreased overall consumer spending (including but not limited to the increase in unemployment caused by the coronavirus pandemic), or the inability to increase menu prices or realize the benefits of menu price increases; risks associated with our increased focus on our digital business, including risks arising from our reliance on third party delivery services, which are heightened during the pendency of government restrictions on dine in restaurant services as a result of the coronavirus pandemic; risks relating to litigation, including possible governmental actions related to food safety incidents and potential class action litigation regarding employment laws, advertising claims or other matters; and other risk factors described from time to time in our SEC reports, including our annual report on Form 10-K and quarterly reports on Form 10-Q, all of which are available on the investor relations page of our website at ir.Chipotle.com.</font>

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk22568764"></a><font style="display: inline;">The following tables provide a reconciliation of non-GAAP financial measures presented in the text above to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;background-color:yellow;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">Adjusted net income is net income excluding expenses related to </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">restaurant asset impairment, corporate restructuring, legal proceedings, stock-</font><font style="display: inline;">based compensation modification expense, and certain other costs. Adjusted general and administrative expense is general and administrative expense excluding transformation expenses, stock-based compensation modification expense, and certain other costs. The non-GAAP effective tax rate is the effective tax rate adjusted to reflect the tax effect of non-GAAP adjustments. Restaurant Level Operating Margin, a non-GAAP financial measure, is equal to the revenues generated by our restaurants less their direct operating costs which consist of food, beverage and packaging, labor, occupancy and other operating costs. This performance measure primarily includes the costs that restaurant level managers can directly control and excludes other operating costs that are essential to conduct our business. &nbsp;Management uses restaurant level operating margin as a measure of restaurant performance. Management believes restaurant level operating margin is useful to investors in that it highlights trends in our core business that may not otherwise be apparent to investors when relying solely on GAAP financial measures. We present these non-GAAP measures in order to facilitate meaningful evaluation of our operating performance across periods. These adjustments are intended to provide greater transparency of underlying performance and to allow investors to evaluate our business on the same basis as our management, which uses these non-GAAP measures in evaluating the company&#x2019;s performance. Our adjusted net income, adjusted diluted earnings per share, adjusted general and administrative expenses, non-GAAP effective tax rate and restaurant level operating margin measures may not be comparable to other companies&#x2019; adjusted measures. These adjustments are not necessarily indicative of what our actual financial performance would have been during the periods presented and should be viewed in addition to, and not as an alternative to, our results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Further details regarding these adjustments are included in the tables below.</font>
